# DSL Reference

All Gherkin steps that match the DSL expressions described here are readily executable by Gwen. The DSL matched is the operation that will be performed at execution time.

:::info The DSL is meant for meta

Feature specs should be declarative and written in the language of your domain and not the Gwen DSL. To encourage this and restrict DSL usage to [meta](/docs/meta) in [Gwen 3](/docs/gwen3), we have toggled the default of the [`gwen.feature.mode`](/docs/settings/reference#gwen-feature-mode) setting from *imperative* to *declarative*.

:::

## Variables

### Given

<details id="name-is-value">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is "<value>"
  ```
  <p>Binds the given value to a name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;value&gt;</code> is the value to bind (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    Given my name is "Gwen"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-value">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-javascript-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by <javascript|js> "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Associates a name with the return value of a JavaScript expression or anonymous function.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to associate</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript|js&gt;</code> is <code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or anonymous function that will return the value (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>For an expression: no <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>For an anonymous function: the syntax is <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code> where body must return a value</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/advanced/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code> or <code>@Lazy</code></Link> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either annotation, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given iso date is defined by js "new Date().toISOString().substring(0, 10)"
     Then iso date should match regex "^\d{4}-([0]\d|1[0-2])-([0-2]\d|3[01])$"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-javascript-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-js-function-applied-to-arg">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by <javascriptRef> applied to "<argument>"
  ```
  <p>Applies a JavaScript function to an argument and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the function result to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascriptRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the javascript function to apply</li>
    <li><code>&lt;argument&gt;</code> argument to apply the function to
      <ul>
        <li>The agrument is referenced in the JavaScript as <code>arguments[0]</code></li>
      </ul>
    </li>

  </ul>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {9}
    Given iso date is defined by js "new Date().toISOString().substring(0, 10)"
      And toDMY is defined by js
          """
          (function(ymd) {
            var parts = ymd.split('-');
            return parts[2] + '/' + parts[1] + '/' + parts[0];
          })(arguments[0])
          """
      And dmy date is defined by toDMY applied to "${iso date}"
     Then dmy date should match regex "^([0-2]\d|3[01])/([0]\d|1[0-2])/\d{4}$"
  ```

  ```gherkin {9}
    Given toMDY is defined by js
          """
          (function(ymd) {
            var months = ['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun', 'Jul', 'Aug', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec'];
            var parts = ymd.split('-');
            return months[parseInt(parts[1]) - 1] + ' ' + parts[2] + ' ' + parts[0];
          })(arguments[0])
          """
      And dmy date is defined by toMDY applied to "2022-04-05"
     Then dmy date should be "Apr 05 2022"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-js-function-applied-to-arg">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.10.1">v3.10.1</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-js-function-applied-to-args-delimited-by">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by <javascriptRef> applied to "<arguments>" delimited by "<delimiter>"
  ```
  <p>Applies a JavaScript function to mutiple arguments using a customer delimiter and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the function result to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascriptRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the javascript function to apply</li>
    <li><code>&lt;arguments&gt;</code> a delimited list of arguments to apply the function to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;delimiter&gt;</code> is the delmiter used in <code>&lt;arguments&gt;</code>
      <ul>
        <li>The 1st agrument is referenced in the JavaScript as <code>arguments[0]</code>, the 2nd argument as <code>arguments[1]</code>, the 3rd as <code>arguments[2]</code> and so on.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {8}
    Given iso date is defined by js "new Date().toISOString().substring(0, 10)"
      And toDMY is defined by js
          """
          (function(y,m,d) {
            return d + '/' + m + '/' + y;
          })(arguments[0], arguments[1], arguments[2])
          """
      And dmy date is defined by toDMY applied to "${iso date}" delimited by "-"
     Then dmy date should match regex "^([0-2]\d|3[01])/([0]\d|1[0-2])/\d{4}$"
  ```
  
  ```gherkin {10}
    Given toISO is defined by js
          """
          (function(m,d,y) {
            var months = ['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun', 'Jul', 'Aug', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec'];
            var mNo = months.indexOf(m) + 1;
            if (mNo < 10) mNo = '0' + mNo;
            return y + '-' + mNo + '-' + d;
          })(arguments[0], arguments[1], arguments[2])
          """
      And iso date is defined by toISO applied to "Apr 05 2022" delimited by " "
     Then iso date should be "2022-04-05"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-js-function-applied-to-args-delimited-by">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.10.0">v3.10.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-in-text-ref-by-regex-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined in <textRef> by regex "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Captures text from a text reference using the given regex expression and associates it with the given name. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the name to associate the captured value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the regex selector expression</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/advanced/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code> or <code>@Lazy</code></Link> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either annotation, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the date is "2021-09-22"
      And the year is defined in the date by regex "(\d{4})"
     Then the year should be "2021"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-in-text-ref-by-regex-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-the-node-type-in-xml-ref-by-xpath-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by the <nodeType> in <xmlRef> by xpath "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Captures content from a referenced XML value using the given XPath expression and associates it with the given name. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the name to associate the captured value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;nodeType&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to capture the text node</li>
        <li><code>node</code> to capture a single node</li>
        <li><code>nodeset</code> to capture multiple nodes</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;xmlRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the XML source
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to XML text, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/advanced/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code> or <code>@Lazy</code></Link> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either annotation, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the xml is "<result><status>passed</status></result>"
      And status is defined by the text in the xml by xpath "//result/status"
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-the-node-type-in-xml-ref-by-xpath-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-in-json-ref-by-json-path-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined in <jsonRef> by json path "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Captures content from a referenced JSON value using the given JSON path expression and associates it with the given name. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the name to associate the captured value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;nodeType&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to capture the text node</li>
        <li><code>node</code> to capture a single node</li>
        <li><code>nodeset</code> to capture multiple nodes</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;sourceRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the XML source
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to XML text, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/advanced/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code> or <code>@Lazy</code></Link> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either annotation, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the json is "{ "status": "passed" }"
      And the status is defined in the json by json path "$.status"
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-in-json-ref-by-json-path-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>


<details id="name-is-defined-by-system-process-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by system process "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Associates a name with the return value of a local system process. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to associated the returned value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the system process that will return the value to assign (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/advanced/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code> or <code>@Lazy</code></Link> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either annotation, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given my hostname is defined by system process "hostname"
     Then my hostname should not be ""
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-system-process-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-system-process-expression-delimited-by-delimiters">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by system process "<expression>" delimited by "<delimiters>"
  ```
  <p>Associates a name with the return value of a delimited local system process. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to associated the returned value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the system process that will return the value to assign (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>Delmiters are required for special cases such as when unbalanced quoted strings are passed as arguments (see example).</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;delmiters&gt;</code> is a regex pattern defining the delimiter(s) used in <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/advanced/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code> or <code>@Lazy</code></Link> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either annotation, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given my message is defined by system process "echo,"quoted text " and orphan quote"" delimited by ","
     Then my message should be ""quoted text " and orphan quote""
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-system-process-expression-delimited-by-delimiters">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-unix-system-process-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by unix system process "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Associates a name with the return value of a local unix system process. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to associated the returned value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the unix system process that will return the value to assign (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/advanced/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code> or <code>@Lazy</code></Link> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either annotation, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  Given a <i>file.csv</i> with content:
  ```
  Word1,Word2,Compound
  basket,ball,basketball
  sun,flower,sunflower
  ```

  The following will print the data and line up each column

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given my table is defined by unix system process "cat file.csv | column -t -s\,"
     Then my table should be 
          """
          Word1   Word2   Compound
          basket  ball    basketball
          sun     flower  sunflower
          """
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-unix-system-process-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.19.0">v3.19.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="name-is-defined-by-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> is defined by file "<filepath>"
  ```
  <p>Associates a name with the contents of a file. The value is resolved every time the name is referenced.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to associated the file contents</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the file (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>
    Optionally accepts the <Link href="/docs/advanced/eager-or-lazy"><code>@Eager</code> or <code>@Lazy</code></Link> annotations.
    <ul>
      <li><code>@Eager</code> immediately evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code></li>
      <li><code>@Lazy</code> evaluates the <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> and binds the result to <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> when it is first referenced</li>
      <li>In the absence of either annotation, <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is evaluated every time <code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is referenced</li>
    </ul>
  </p>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    Given the content is defined by file "path/to/file.txt"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-is-defined-by-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.11.0">v1.11.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

### When

<details id="i-capture-text-ref-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <textRef> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the referenced text and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the username is "Gwen"
     When I capture the username as my username
     Then my username should be the username
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-text-ref-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-name-by-javascript-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <name> by <javascript|js> "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Captures the return value of a JavaScript expression or anonymous function and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the returned value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript|js&gt;</code> is <code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or anonymous function that will return the value (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>For an expression: no <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>For an anonymous function: the syntax is <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code> where body must return a value</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
     When I capture iso date by js "new Date().toISOString().substring(0, 10)"
     Then iso date should match regex "^\d{4}-([0]\d|1[0-2])-([0-2]\d|3[01])$"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-name-by-javascript-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-text-in-text-ref-by-regex-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the text in <textRef> by regex "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the referenced text using the given regex expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the regex selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the date is "2021-09-22"
     When I capture the text in the date by regex "(\d{4})" as the year
     Then the year should be "2021"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-text-in-text-ref-by-regex-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-node-type-in-xml-ref-by-xpath-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the <nodeType> in <xmlRef> by xpath "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures XML content from a referenced XML string using the given XPath expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;nodeType&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to capture the text node</li>
        <li><code>node</code> to capture a single node</li>
        <li><code>nodeset</code> to capture multiple nodes</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;xmlRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the XML text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an XML text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the xml is "<result><status>passed</status></result>"
     When I capture the text in the xml by xpath "//result/status" as the status
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-node-type-in-xml-ref-by-xpath-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-content-in-json-ref-by-json-path-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the content in <jsonRef> by json path "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures JSON content from a referenced JSON string using the given JSON Path expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;jsonRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the source JSON source
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a JSON text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON selector</Link> expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the json is "{ "status": "passed" }"
     When I capture the content in the json by json path "$.status" as the status
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-content-in-json-ref-by-json-path-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-compared-to-text-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the similarity score of <textRef> compared to "<text>"[ ignoring case] as <name>
  ```
  <p>Compares a text reference with a text value for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm and binds the calculated score to <code>name</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing a text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> is the text to compare <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> against</li>
    <li><code> ignoring case</code> ignores case if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the calculated score to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2-4}
    Given the phrase is "Hello world!"
     When I capture the similarity score of the phrase compared to "Hello world" as similarity score 1
      And I capture the similarity score of the phrase compared to "hello world" as similarity score 2
      And I capture the similarity score of the phrase compared to "hello world" ignoring case as similarity score 3
     Then similarity score 1 should be "0.9411764705882353"
      And similarity score 2 should be "0.8235294117647058"
      And similarity score 3 should be "0.9411764705882353"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-compared-to-text-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.0">v3.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-1-compared-to-text-ref-2-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the similarity score of <textRef1> compared to <textRef2>[ ignoring case] as <name>
  ```
  <p>Compares a text reference with another for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm and binds the calculated score to <code>name</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef1&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing a text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef2&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the second text reference to compare &lt;textRef1&gt; against
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code> ignoring case</code> ignores case if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the calculated score to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3-4}
    Given phrase 1 is "Hello world!"
      And phrase 2 is "hello world"
     When I capture the similarity score of phrase 1 compared to phrase 2 as similarity score 1
      And I capture the similarity score of phrase 1 compared to phrase 2 ignoring case as similarity score 2
     Then similarity score 1 should be "0.8235294117647058"
      And similarity score 2 should be "0.9411764705882353"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-1-compared-to-text-ref-2-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.0">v3.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-compared-to-text">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the similarity score of <textRef> compared to "<text>"[ ignoring case]
  ```
  <p>Compares a text reference with a text value for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm and binds the calculated score to the <code>similarity score</code> attribute in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing a text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> is the text to compare <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> against</li>
    <li><code> ignoring case</code> ignores case if included</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the phrase is "Hello world!"
     When I capture the similarity score of the phrase compared to "Hello world"
     Then similarity score should be "0.9411764705882353"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-compared-to-text">Link</Link></div>

  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-1-compared-to-text-ref-2">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the similarity score of <textRef1> compared to <textRef2>[ ignoring case]
  ```
  <p>Compares a text reference with another for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm and binds the calculated score to the <code>similarity score</code> attribute in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef1&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing a text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef2&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the second text reference to compare &lt;textRef1&gt; against
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code> ignoring case</code> ignores case if included</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given phrase 1 is "Hello world!"
      And phrase 2 is "hello world"
     When I capture the similarity score of phrase 1 compared to phrase 2
     Then similarity score should be "0.8235294117647058"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-similarity-score-of_text-ref-1-compared-to-text-ref-2">Link</Link></div>

<details id="i-base64-decode-text-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I base64 decode <textRef>
  ```
  <p>Base64 decodes the text reference and binds the result to the same name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to decode
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the data is "c29tZSBiaW5hcnkgZGF0YQ=="
     When I base64 decode the data
     Then the data should be "some binary data"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-base64-decode-text-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-base64-decode-text-ref-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I base64 decode <textRef> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Base64 decodes the text reference and binds the result to the give name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to decode
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the decoded value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the encoded data is "c29tZSBiaW5hcnkgZGF0YQ=="
     When I base64 decode the encoded data as the decoded data
     Then the decoded data should be "some binary data"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-base64-decode-text-ref-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

### Then

<details id="text-ref-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] be blank
  ```

  <p>Checks whether or not the text reference matches a blank string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>

  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] be blank with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] be blank with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to check
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {6}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I enter "Get the milk" in the todo field
      And I capture my todo list as current items
     Then current items should not be blank
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#text-ref-should-match-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.26.0">v3.26.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="text-ref-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```

  <p>Checks whether or not the text reference matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>

  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> "<expression>" with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> "<expression>" with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to check
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {6}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I enter "Get the milk" in the todo field
      And I capture my todo list as current items
     Then current items should contain "Get the milk"
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#text-ref-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="text-ref-should-match-expression-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the value of a variable or setting matches a referenced expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>

  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;variable&gt;</code> is the name of the variable or setting to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an expression value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {7}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
      And my item is "Feed the cat"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I enter my item in the todo field
      And I capture my todo list as current items
     Then current items should contain my item
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#text-ref-should-match-expression-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>


<details id="xml-ref-at-xpath-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not>] be blank
  ```
  
  <p>Extracts text from the referenced XML value using the given XPath and checks whether or not it matches a blank string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not>] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not>] be blank with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not>] be blank with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;xmlRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the XML source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an XML text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>path</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the xml is "<result><status>passed</status></result>"
     Then the xml at xpath "//result/status" should not be blank
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#xml-ref-at-xpath-should-match-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.26.0">v3.26.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="xml-ref-at-xpath-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not>] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Extracts text from the referenced XML value using the given XPath and checks that it matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not>] <match> "<expression>"  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not>] <match> "<expression>" with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <xmlRef> at xpath "<path>" should[ not>] <match> "<expression>" with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;xmlRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the XML source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an XML text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>path</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the xml is "<result><status>passed</status></result>"
     Then the xml at xpath "//result/status" should be "passed"
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#xml-ref-at-xpath-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.6.0">v2.6.0</Link></div>

<details id="json-ref-at-json-path-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <jsonRef> at json path "<path>" should[ not>] be blank
  ```
  
  <p>Extracts text from the referenced JSON value using the given JSON path and checks whether or not it matches a blank string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <jsonRef> at json path "<path>" should[ not>] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <jsonRef> at json path "<path>" should[ not>] be blank with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <jsonRef> at json path "<path>" should[ not>] be blank with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;jsonRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the JSON source text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a JSON text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>path</code> is the <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON path</Link> selector expression</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
      Given the json is "{ "status": "passed" }"
       Then the json at json path "$.status" should not be blank
  ```

<details id="json-ref-at-json-path-should-match-expression">


  </summary>

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>

      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a JSON text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>path</code> is the <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON path</Link> selector expression</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

<details id="name-should-be-absent">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be absent
  ```

  <p>Checks that a named binding is absent from the current scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be absent  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be absent with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be absent with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the binding to check</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    Then this should be absent
  ```
  
  or equivalently (as of v3.29.0)

  ```gherkin
    Then that should not be defined
  ```
