<details id="name-should-be-defined">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <name> should[ not] be defined
  ```

  <p>Checks whether or not a named binding exists in the current scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message:</p>

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be defined  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be defined with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <name> should be defined with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the binding to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the check (for absence/non existence)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  To check for the presence of a binding
  
  ```gherkin
    Then this should be defined
  ```

  To check for the absence of a binding
  
  ```gherkin
    Then that should not be defined
  ```

  or equivalently

  ```gherkin
    Then that should be absent
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#name-should-be-defined">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.29.0">v3.29.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>


<details id="text-ref-should-be-similar-to-text">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to "<text>"[ ignoring case]
  ```

  <p>Compares a text reference with a text value for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to "<text>"[ ignoring case]  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to "<text>"[ ignoring case] with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to "<text>"[ ignoring case] with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing a text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>match</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>be less than</code> for less than match</li>
        <li><code>be at most</code> for less than or equal to match</li>
        <li><code>be more than</code> for greater than match</li>
        <li><code>be at least</code> for greater than or equal to match</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> is the text to compare <code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> against</li>
    <li><code> ignoring case</code> ignores case if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  The calculated similarity score is implicity bound to the <code>similarity score</code> attribute in the global scope.
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {2-7}
    Given the phrase is "Hello world!"
     Then the phrase should be more than 90% similar to "Hello world"
      And the phrase should be at least 90% similar to "hello world" ignoring case
      And the phrase should be 94.12% similar to "Hello world"
      And the phrase should be 94.12% similar to "hello world" ignoring case
      And the phrase should be 82.35% similar to "hello world"
      And the phrase should not be less than 90% similar to "Hello world"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#text-ref-should-be-similar-to-text">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.0">v3.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="text-ref-1-should-be-similar-to-text-ref-2">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <textRef1> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to <textRef2>[ ignoring case]
  ```

  <p>Compares a text reference with another for similarity using the DSC (Dice Similarity Coefficient) algorithm.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef1> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to <textRef2>[ ignoring case]  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef1> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to <textRef2>[ ignoring case] with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <textRef1> should[ not] <match> <percentage>% similar to <textRef2>[ ignoring case] with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef1&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the first text reference
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>match</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>be less than</code> for less than match</li>
        <li><code>be at most</code> for less than or equal to match</li>
        <li><code>be more than</code> for greater than match</li>
        <li><code>be at least</code> for greater than or equal to match</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;percentage&gt;</code> is a percentage number between 0 and 100 (internally rounded to 2 decimal places)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef2&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the second text reference to compare <code>&lt;textRef1&gt;</code> against
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code> ignoring case</code> ignores case if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  The calculated similarity score is implicity bound to the <code>similarity score</code> attribute in the global scope.
  <p>Examples</p>

  ```gherkin {4-9}
    Given phrase 1 is "Hello world!"
      And phrase 2 is "Hello world"
      And phrase 3 is "hello world"
     Then phrase 1 should be more than 90% similar to phrase 2
      And phrase 1 should be at least 90% similar to phrase 2 ignoring case
      And phrase 1 should be 94.12% similar to phrase 2
      And phrase 1 should be 94.12% similar to phrase 3 ignoring case
      And phrase 1 should be 82.35% similar to phrase 3
      And phrase 1 should not be less than 90% similar to phrase 2
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#text-ref-1-should-be-similar-to-text-ref-2">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.0">v3.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

## Web pages

### Given

<details id="the-page-url-is-url">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the <page> url is "<url>"
  ```
  <p>Puts the given page into scope and binds the given URL to it.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;page&gt;</code> is the name of the page</li>
    <li><code>&lt;url&gt;</code> is the page URL (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given the todo page url is "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-page-url-is-url">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.41.0">v2.41.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-am-on-the-page">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I am on the <page>
  ```
  <p>Puts the given page into scope and makes its bindings avaialble.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;page&gt;</code> is a page name</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I am on the todo page
      And the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-am-on-the-page">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

### When

<details id="i-navigate-to-the-page">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I navigate to the <page>
  ```

  <p>Navigates the browser to the URL bound to the given page and puts the page into scope. Starts a new browser window if one is not open.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;page&gt;</code> is the name of the page to navigate to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the todo page url is "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     When I navigate to the todo page
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-navigate-to-the-page">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-navigate-to-url">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I navigate to "<url>"
  ```

  <p>Navigates the browser to the given URL. Starts a new browser window if one is not open.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;url&gt;</code> is the URL to navigate to (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-navigate-to-url">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-current-url">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the current URL
  ```
  
  <p>Captures the current browser URL and binds it as <code>the current URL</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    When I capture the current URL
     And I navigate to "${the current URL}?q=gwen"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-current-url">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-current-url-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the current URL as <name>
  ```
  
  <p>Captures the current browser URL and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured URL to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    When I capture the current URL as the base URL
     And I navigate to "${the base URL}?q=gwen"
    Then the current URL should start with the base URL
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-current-url-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-text-in-the-current-url-by-regex-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the text in the current URL by regex "<expression>" as <name>
  ```

  <p>Extracts a substring from the current browser URL using the given regex and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the regex expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured substring to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    When I capture the text in the current URL by regex "q=([^&]*)" as q
    Then q should be "gwen"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-text-in-the-current-url-by-regex-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-refresh-the-current-page">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I refresh the current page
  ```

  <p>Refreshes the current page in the browser.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I refresh the current page
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-refresh-the-current-page">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

### Then

<details id="the-current-url-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] be blank
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the current browser URL matches a blank string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] be blank with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] be blank with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
    Then the current URL should not be blank
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-current-url-should-match-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.26.0">v3.26.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="the-current-url-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the current browser URL matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] <match> "<expression>"  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] <match> "<expression>" with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] <match> "<expression>" with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2,3}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
    Then the current URL should contain "todomvc.com"
     And the current URL should not contain "other.com"
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-current-url-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="the-current-url-should-match-expression-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the current URL in the browser matches a referenced expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the current URL should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an expression value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4,5}
    Given my domain is "todomvc.com"
      And some other domain is "someother.com"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     Then the current URL should contain my domain
      And the current URL should not contain some other domain
  ```

    <div><Link to="#the-current-url-should-match-expression-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="the-page-title-should-match-blank">

  <p>Checks whether or not the title of the current page matches a blank string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>

<details id="the-page-title-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the page title should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the title of the current page in the browser matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the page title should[ not] <match> "<expression>"  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the page title should[ not] <match> "<expression>" with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the page title should[ not] <match> "<expression>" with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON path</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
    Then the page title should contain "TodoMVC"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-page-title-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="the-page-title-should-match-expression-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the page title should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  <p>Checks whether or not the title of the current page in the browser matches a referenced expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the page title should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the page title should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the page title should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON path</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an expression value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the app name is "TodoMVC"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     Then the page title should contain the app name
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-page-title-should-match-expression-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-scroll-to-the-top-or-bottom-of-page">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I scroll to the <top|bottom> of the page
  ```
  <p>Scrolls to the top or bottom of the current page.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;top|bottom&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>top</code> to scroll to the top of the page</li>
        <li><code>bottom</code> to scroll to the bottom of the page</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I scroll to the bottom of the page
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-scroll-to-the-top-or-bottom-of-page">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.20.1">v3.20.1</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

## Web elements

### Given

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>"
  ```

  <p>Binds a selector for a web element to the current scope with a default lookup timeout.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-with-no-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" with no <wait|timeout>
  ```

  <p>Binds a selector for a web element to the current scope with no lookup timeout.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given the todo field can be located by css ".new-todo" with no lookup timeout
     When I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-with-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```

  <p>Binds a selector for a web element to the current scope with a given lookup timeout.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given the todo field can be located by css ".new-todo" with 5 second timeout
     When I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
  ```

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-at-index">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" at index <index>
  ```

  <p>Binds an indexed selector for a web element to the current scope with a default lookup timeout.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;index&gt;</code> is the index of the element to select in list returned by <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given the first item can be located by css ".todo-list label" at index 0
     Then the first item should contain "Walk the dog"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-at-index">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.28.0">v2.28.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

  <p>Binds an indexed selector for a web element to the current scope with no lookup timeout.</p>
  </summary>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-at-index-with-timeout">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" at index <index> with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```

    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>

    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
     Then the first item should contain "Walk the dog"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-at-index-with-timeout">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-in-other-element-at-index">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" at index <index> in <otherElement>
  ```

  <p>Binds an indexed selector for a web element (contained in another) to the current scope with a default lookup timeout.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;index&gt;</code> is the index of the element to select in list returned by <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code> is the name of the web element that this one is relative to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the count info can be located by class "todo-count"
      And the count unit can be located by tag "span" at index 1 in the count info
     Then the count unit should contain "item"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-in-other-element-at-index">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.28.0">v2.28.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-at-index-in-other-element-with-no-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" at index <index> in <otherElement> with no <wait|timeout>
  ```

  <p>Binds an indexed selector for a web element (contained in another) to the current scope with no lookup timeout.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;index&gt;</code> is the index of the element to select in list returned by <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code> is the name of the web element that this one is relative to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the count info can be located by class "todo-count"
      And the count unit can be located by tag "span" at index 1 in the count info with no wait
     Then the count unit should contain "item"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-at-index-in-other-element-with-no-timeout">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.28.0">v2.28.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-at-index-in-other-element-with-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" at index <index> in <otherElement>  with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```

  <p>Binds an indexed selector for a web element (contained in another) to the current scope with a given lookup timeout.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;index&gt;</code> is the index of the element to select in list returned by <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code> is the name of the web element that this one is relative to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

 ```gherkin {2}
    Given the count info can be located by class "todo-count"
      And the count unit can be located by tag "span" at index 1 in the count info with 5 second wait
     Then the count unit should contain "item"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-at-index-in-other-element-with-timeout">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.28.0">v2.28.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-with-fallbacks">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by
    | selector     | expression     |
    | <selector 1> | <expression 1> |
    | <selector 2> | <expression 2> |
    |      ..      |       ..       |
    | <selector n> | <expression n> |
  ```

  <p>
    Binds primary and fallback selectors for a web element to the current scope with a default lookup timeout.
    Lookups will be attempted in the order specified until one succeeds.
  </p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector n&gt;</code> is the nth selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression n&gt;</code> is the nth selector expression</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1-5}
    Given the todo field can be located by
          | selector | expression  |
          | name     | todo-field  |
          | css      | .todo input |
          | class    | new-todo    |
     When I type "Feed the cat" in the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-with-fallbacks">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.11.0">v2.11.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-with-fallbacks-at-index">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located at index <index> by
    | selector     | expression     |
    | <selector 1> | <expression 1> |
    | <selector 2> | <expression 2> |
    |      ..      |       ..       |
    | <selector n> | <expression n> |
  ```

  <p>
    Binds indexed primary and fallback selectors for a web element to the current scope with a default lookup timeout.
    Lookups will be attempted in the order specified until one succeeds.
  </p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector n&gt;</code> is the nth selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression n&gt;</code> is the nth selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;index&gt;</code> is the index of the element to select in list returned by <code>&lt;expression n&gt;</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1-5}
    Given the second item can be located at index 1 by
          | selector | expression       |
          | name     | todo-label       |
          | class    | todo-label       |
          | css      | .todo-list label |
     Then the second item should contain "Feed the cat"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">

    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.28.0">v2.28.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-with-fallbacks-at-index-with-no-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located at index <index> with no <wait|timeout> by
    | selector     | expression     |
    | <selector 1> | <expression 1> |
    | <selector 2> | <expression 2> |
    |      ..      |       ..       |
    | <selector n> | <expression n> |
  ```

  <p>
    Binds indexed primary and fallback selectors for a web element to the current scope with no lookup timeout.
    Lookups will be attempted in the order specified until one succeeds.
  </p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector n&gt;</code> is the nth selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression n&gt;</code> is the nth selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;index&gt;</code> is the index of the element to select in list returned by <code>&lt;expression n&gt;</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1-5}
    Given the second item can be located at index 1 with no lookup timeout by
          | selector | expression       |
          | name     | todo-label       |
          | class    | todo-label       |
          | css      | .todo-list label |
     Then the second item should contain "Feed the cat"
  ```

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-with-fallbacks-at-index-with-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located at index <index> with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout> by
    | selector     | expression     |
    | <selector 1> | <expression 1> |
    | <selector 2> | <expression 2> |
    |      ..      |       ..       |
    | <selector n> | <expression n> |
  ```

  <p>
    Binds indexed primary and fallback selectors for a web element to the current scope with a given lookup timeout.
    Lookups will be attempted in the order specified until one succeeds.
  </p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector n&gt;</code> is the nth selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression n&gt;</code> is the nth selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;index&gt;</code> is the index of the element to select in list returned by <code>&lt;expression n&gt;</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1-5}
    Given the second item can be located at index 1 with 5 second timeout by
          | selector | expression       |
          | name     | todo-label       |
          | class    | todo-label       |
          | css      | .todo-list label |
     Then the second item should contain "Feed the cat"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-with-fallbacks-at-index-with-timeout">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.28.0">v2.28.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-actioned-by-javascript">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be <actioned> by <javascript|js> "<javascript>"
  ```
  <p>Registers a javascript action on an element. When the action is performed, then the javascript will execute in place of the default behaviour.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to register the action on</li>
    <li><code>&lt;actioned&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>clicked</code> to perform the action when the element is clicked</li>
        <li><code>right clicked</code> to perform the action when the element is right clicked, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>double clicked</code> to perform the action when the element is double clicked, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>submitted</code> to perform the action when the form element is submitted</li>
        <li><code>checked</code> (or <code>ticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to perform the action when the checkbox element is ticked</li>
        <li><code>unchecked</code> (or <code>unticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to perform the action when the checkbox element is unticked</li>
        <li><code>selected</code> to perform the action when a dropdown option is selected in the element</li>
        <li><code>deselected</code> to perform the action when a mutli-select dropdown option is deselected in the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>typed</code> to perform the action when text is typed into the element</li>
        <li><code>entered</code> to perform the action when text is entered into the element</li>
        <li><code>tabbed</code> to perform the action when the tab key is pressed in the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.17.1">v2.17.1</Link></li>
        <li><code>cleared</code> to perform the action when the text is cleared in the element</li>
        <li><code>moved to</code> to perform the action when the focus is moved to the element</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript|js&gt;</code> is <code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> , since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or anonymous function that will perform the desired action (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>The reference to the element will be provided to the javascript through an implicit object named <code>element</code>.</li>
        <li>For an expression: no <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>For an anonymous function: the syntax is <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code> where body must return a value</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the submit button can be located by css ".submit"
      And the submit button can be clicked by js "element.click()"
     When I click the submit button
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-actioned-by-javascript">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.8.0">v1.8.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Relative Locators

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-relative-to-other-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" <relativeTo> <otherElement>
  ```

  <p>Binds a selector for a web element (relative to another) to the current scope with a default lookup timeout.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;relativeTo&gt;</code> is one of
      <ul>
        <li><code>in</code> to select element contained in <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
        <li>Or since <Link to="/docs/gwen3">Gwen 3</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><code>above</code> to select element above <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>below</code> to select element below <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>to left of</code> to select element to the left of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>to right of</code> to select element to the right of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>near</code> to select element near <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>near and within &lt;noOfPixels&gt; pixel[s] of</code> to select element near and within a given number of pixels of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code>
              <ul>
                <li>Where <code>&lt;noOfPixels&gt;</code> is a postive integer denoting a number of pixels (max proximity to <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code>)</li>
              </ul>
            </li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code> is the name of the web element that this one is relative to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the button can be located by tag "button"
      And the left field can be located by css "input" to left of the button 
     When I navigate to "https://chercher.tech/practice/relative-locators"
      And I type "I am left of the button" in the left field
     Then the left field should contain "I am left of the button"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-relative-to-other-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.1.0">v1.1.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-relative-to-other-element-with-no-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" <relativeTo> <otherElement> with no <wait|timeout>
  ```

  <p>Binds a selector for a web element (relative to another) to the current scope with no lookup timeout.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;relativeTo&gt;</code> is one of
      <ul>
        <li><code>in</code> to select element contained in <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
        <li>Or since <Link to="/docs/gwen3">Gwen 3</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><code>above</code> to select element above <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>below</code> to select element below <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>to left of</code> to select element to the left of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>to right of</code> to select element to the right of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>near</code> to select element near <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>near and within &lt;noOfPixels&gt; pixel[s] of</code> to select element near and within a given number of pixels of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code>
              <ul>
                <li>Where <code>&lt;noOfPixels&gt;</code> is a postive integer denoting a number of pixels (max proximity to <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code>)</li>
              </ul>
            </li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code> is the name of the web element that this one is relative to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the button can be located by tag "button"
      And the right field can be located by css "input" to right of the button with no wait
     When I navigate to "https://chercher.tech/practice/relative-locators"
      And I type "I am right of the button" in the right field
     Then the right field should contain "I am right of the button"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-relative-to-other-element-with-no-timeout">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"><Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/">Learn more</Link></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.19.0">v2.19.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-can-be-located-by-selector-expression-relative-to-other-element-with-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> can be located by <selector> "<expression>" <relativeTo> <otherElement>  with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```

  <p>Binds a selector for a web element (relative to another) to the current scope with a given lookup timeout.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the web element name</li>
    <li><code>&lt;selector&gt;</code> is the selector type, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>id</code> for selecting by id attribute</li>
        <li><code>name</code> for selecting by name attribute</li>
        <li><code>tag name</code> (or <code>tag</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by tag name</li>
        <li><code>css selector</code> (or <code>css</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by css expression</li>
        <li><code>class name</code> (or <code>class</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting by class attribute</li>
        <li><code>xpath</code> for selecting by XPath</li>
        <li><code>link text</code> for selecting by link text</li>
        <li><code>partial link text</code> for selecting by partial link text</li>
        <li><code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>) for selecting <Link to="https://gweninterpreter.wordpress.com/2019/08/13/locating-web-elements-with-gwen/#byJavaScript">by JavaScript</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;relativeTo&gt;</code> is one of
      <ul>
        <li><code>in</code> to select element contained in <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
        <li>Or since <Link to="/docs/gwen3">Gwen 3</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><code>above</code> to select element above <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>below</code> to select element below <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>to left of</code> to select element to the left of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>to right of</code> to select element to the right of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>near</code> to select element near <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code></li>
            <li><code>near and within &lt;noOfPixels&gt; pixel[s] of</code> to select element near and within a given number of pixels of <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code>
              <ul>
                <li>Where <code>&lt;noOfPixels&gt;</code> is a postive integer denoting a number of pixels (max proximity to <code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code>)</li>
              </ul>
            </li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;otherElement&gt;</code> is the name of the web element that this one is relative to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

 ```gherkin {2}
    Given the button can be located by tag "button"
      And the above field can be located by css "input" above the button with 5 second wait
     When I navigate to "https://chercher.tech/practice/relative-locators"
      And I type "I am above the button" in the above field
     Then the above field should contain "I am above the button"
  ```
