### When

<details id="i-click-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <click|right click|double click> <element>
  ```
  <p>Clicks a web element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;click|right click|double click&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>click</code> to click the element</li>
        <li><code>right click</code> to right click the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>double click</code> to double click the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to click</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the start button can be located by name "commit"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
      And I click the start button
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-click-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-click-element-of-context">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <click|right click|double click> <element> of <context>
  ```
  <p>Clicks a context sensitive web element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;click|right click|double click&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>click</code> to click the element</li>
        <li><code>right click</code> to right click the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>double click</code> to double click the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to click</li>
    <li><code>&lt;context&gt;</code> is the context element to focus into (in order to click <code>&lt;element&gt;</code>)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the menu item can be located by id "menu-item-id"
      And the action button can be located by id "action-button-id"
     When I click the action button of the menu item
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-click-element-of-context">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-modifier-keys-click-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <modifierKeys> <click|right click|double click> <element>
  ```
  <p>Holds down the specified modifier keys and clicks an element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;modifierKeys&gt;</code> is a <code>+</code> separated list of modifier keys to hold down during the click
      <ul>
        <li>Modifier keys can be single keyboard characters or any supported <Link to="https://seleniumhq.github.io/selenium/docs/api/java/org/openqa/selenium/Keys.html">key constants</Link></li>
        <li><i>Node:</i> Keys behave differently on different platforms</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;click|right click|double click&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>click</code> to click the element</li>
        <li><code>right click</code> to right click the element</li>
        <li><code>double click</code> to double click the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to click</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the button can be located by tag "button"
      And I COMMAND+SHIFT click the button
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-modifier-keys-click-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-tick-or-until-checkbox">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <check|uncheck|tick|untick> <checkbox>
  ```
  <p>Ticks or unticks a checkbox element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;check|uncheck|tick|untick&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>check</code> (or <code>tick</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to tick the checkbox element</li>
        <li><code>uncheck</code> (or <code>untick</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to untick the checkbox element</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;checkbox&gt;</code> is the name of the checkbox element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the email checkbox can be located by id "checkbox1"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I tick the email checkbox
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-tick-or-until-checkbox">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-submit-form">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I submit <form>
  ```
  <p>Submits a web form.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;form&gt;</code> is the name of the form to submit</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the form can be located by name "contactform"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I submit the form
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-submit-form">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-move-to-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I move to <element>
  ```
  <p>Moves to a web element and gives it the focus.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to move to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the surname field can be located by id "surname"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I move to the surname field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-move-to-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-enter-or-type-text-in-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <enter|type> "<text>" in <element>
  ```
  <p>Enters or types text into a web element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;enter|type&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>enter</code> to send the text to the field followed by the enter key</li>
        <li><code>type</code> to send the text to the field only (without trailing enter key)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> is the text to send to the field</li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the field to send the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-enter-or-type-text-in-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-enter-or-type-text-ref-in-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <enter|type> <textRef> in <element>
  ```
  <p>Enters or types a text reference value into a web element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;enter|type&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>enter</code> to send the text to the field followed by the enter key</li>
        <li><code>type</code> to send the text to the field only (without trailing enter key)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to send to the field
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the field to send the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my item is "Walk the dog"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I enter my item in the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-enter-or-type-text-ref-in-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-append-text-to-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I append "<text>" to <element>
  ```
  <p>Appends the given text to the current text value of an element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> is the text to append</li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is name of the element to append the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the search field can be located by name "q"
     When I navigate to "https://google.com"
      And I type "Gwen" in the search field
      And I append " automation" to the search field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-append-text-to-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.18.0">v2.18.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-append-text-ref-to-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I append <textRef> to <element>
  ```
  <p>Appends the given referenced text to the current text value of an element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to append to the element
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is name of the element to append the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the search field can be located by name "q"
      And my additional search term is " automation"
     When I navigate to "https://google.com"
      And I type "Gwen" in the search field
      And I append my additional search term to the search field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-append-text-ref-to-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.18.0">v2.18.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-press-enter-or-tab-in-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I press <enter|tab> in <element>
  ```
  <p>Send the enter or tab key to a web element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;enter|tab&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>enter</code> to send the enter key</li>
        <li><code>tab</code> to send the tab key</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to send the key to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the surname field can be located by id "surname"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I press tab in the surname field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-press-enter-or-tab-in-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-send-keys-to-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I send "<keys>" to <element>
  ```
  <p>Sends a sequence of keys to an element (for emulating keyboard shortcuts).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;keys&gt;</code> is a <code>,</code> or <code>+</code> (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link>) separated list of keys to send.
      <ul>
        <li>Keys can be single keyboard characters or any supported <Link to="https://seleniumhq.github.io/selenium/docs/api/java/org/openqa/selenium/Keys.html">key constants</Link></li>
        <li><i>Note:</i> Keys behave differently on different platforms</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to send the keys to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4,5,7,8}
    Given the search field can be located by name "q"
     When I navigate to "https://google.com"
      And I type "Gwen automation" in the search field
      And I send "COMMAND+A" to the search field
      And I send "COMMAND+C" to the search field
      And I clear the search field
      And I send "COMMAND+V" to the search field
      And I send "ARROW_DOWN" to the search field
      And I press enter in the search field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-send-keys-to-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-insert-a-new-line-in-textarea">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I insert a new line in <textarea>
  ```
  <p>Inserts a new line into a textarea element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;textarea&gt;</code> is the name of the textarea element to insert the new line into</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4,6}
    Given the more field can be located by tag "textarea"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I type "Hi," in the more field
      And I insert a new line in the more field
      And I type "I like Gwen." in the more field
      And I insert a new line in the more field
      And I type "Bye!" in the more field
     Then the more field should contain
          """
          Hi,
          I like Gwen.
          Bye!
          """
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-insert-a-new-line-in-textarea">Link</Link></div>

  </div>
</details>

  ```gherkin
  I clear <element>
  ```

<details id="i-select-or-deselect-the-position-option-in-dropdown">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <select|deselect> the <position><st|nd|rd|th> option in <dropdown>
  ```
  <p>Selects an option in a dropdown by position.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;select|deselect&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>select</code> to select the option</li>
        <li><code>deselect</code> to deselect the option, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><i>Note</i>: Deselect will only work for multi-select dropdowns.</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;position&gt;</code> is the position number of the option(1 for first position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;st|nd|rd|th&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>st</code> if the position number ends in 1</li>
        <li><code>nd</code> if the position number ends in 2</li>
        <li><code>rd</code> if the position number ends in 3</li>
        <li><code>th</code> if the position number is greater than 3</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select the 2nd option in the age dropdown
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-select-or-deselect-the-position-option-in-dropdown">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-select-or-deselect-option-in-dropdown">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <select|deselect> "<option>" in <dropdown>
  ```
  <p>Selects an option in a dropdown by displayed text.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;select|deselect&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>select</code> to select the option</li>
        <li><code>deselect</code> to deselect the option, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><i>Note</i>: Deselect will only work for multi-select dropdowns.</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;option&gt;</code> is the displayed option text</li>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select "18" in the age dropdown
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-select-or-deselect-option-in-dropdown">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-select-or-deselect-option-ref-in-dropdown">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <select|deselect> <optionRef> in <dropdown>
  ```
  <p>Selects an option in a dropdown by a displayed text reference.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;select|deselect&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>select</code> to select the option</li>
        <li><code>deselect</code> to deselect the option, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link>
          <ul>
            <li><i>Note</i>: Deselect will only work for multi-select dropdowns.</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;optionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the displayed option text
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
      And my age is "24"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select my age in the age dropdown
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-select-or-deselect-option-ref-in-dropdown">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

          <ul>
            <li><i>Note</i>: Deselect will only work for multi-select dropdowns.</li>
          </ul>
        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;option&gt;</code> is the hidden option value</li>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element</li>
  </ul>

  <p>Selects an option in a dropdown by hidden value reference.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>

    <li><code>&lt;select|deselect&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>

        </li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;optionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the hidden option value


<details id="i-drag-and-drop-source-element-to-target-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I drag and drop <sourceElement> to <targetElement>
  ```
  <p>Drags and drops a source element onto a target element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;sourceElement&gt;</code> is the name of the source element to drag</li>
    <li><code>&lt;targetElement&gt;</code> is the name of the target element to drop the <code>&lt;sourceElement&gt;</code> into</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the box can be located by xpath "//*[@id='credit2']/a"
      And the cell can be located by xpath "//*[@id='bank']/li"
     When I navigate to "http://demo.guru99.com/test/drag_drop.html"
      And I capture the box as the box text
      And I drag and drop the box to the cell
     Then the cell should contain "${the box text}"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-drag-and-drop-source-element-to-target-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.17.0">v2.17.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <element>
  ```
  <p>Captures the text value of an element and binds it to the element name in the global scode.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to capture the text of</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I capture the heading
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>

<details id="i-capture-element-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <element> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the text value of an element and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to capture the text of</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}

     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
  ```

</details>

<details id="i-capture-dropdown">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <dropdown> <text|value>
  ```
  <p>Captures the selected text or value of a dropdown element and binds it to the element name in the global scode.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element to capture the text or value of</li>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to captured the displayed text of the selection</li>
        <li><code>value</code> to captured the option value of the selection</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I capture the age dropdown text
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-dropdown">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-dropdown-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <dropdown> <text|value> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the selected text or value of a dropdown element and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the name of the dropdown element to capture the text or value of</li>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to captured the displayed text of the selection</li>
        <li><code>value</code> to captured the option value of the selection</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I capture the age dropdown text my age
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-dropdown-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-text-in-element-by-regex-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the text in <element> by regex "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures text content from a web element using the given regex expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to capture text from</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the regex selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # assuming a web element contains date: 2021-09-22
    Given the date field can be located by class "date"
     When I capture the text in the date field by regex "(\d{4})" as the year
     Then the year should be "2021"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-text-in-element-by-regex-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-node-type-in-element-by-xpath-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the <nodeType> in <element> by xpath "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures XML content from a web element using the given XPath expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;nodeType&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to capture the text node</li>
        <li><code>node</code> to capture a single node</li>
        <li><code>nodeset</code> to capture multiple nodes</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element containing the XML content</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the XPath selector expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # assuming a web element contains xml: <result><status>passed</status></result>
    Given the xml web element can be located by id "xml"
     When I capture the text in the xml web element by xpath "//result/status" as the status
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-node-type-in-element-by-xpath-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-content-in-element-by-json-path-expression-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the content in <element> by json path "<expression>" as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures JSON content from a web element using the given JSON Path expression and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element containing the JSON content</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON selector</Link> expression</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the captured value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # assuming a web element contains json: { "status": "passed" }
    Given the json web element can be located by id "json"
     When I capture the content in the json web element by json path "$.status" as the status
     Then the status should be "passed"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-content-in-element-by-json-path-expression-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-name-of-element-by-javascript-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture <name> <of|on|in> <element> by <javascript|js> "<javascript>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a JavaScript expression or anonymous function on an element and binds the result to the given name.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the javascript return value to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;of|on|in&gt;</code> is <code>of</code>, <code>on</code> or <code>in</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to execute the javascript on</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript|js&gt;</code> is <code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript&gt;</code> is the JavaScript expression or anonymous function to execute (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>The reference to the element will be provided to the javascript through an implicit object named <code>element</code>.</li>
        <li>For an expression: no <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>For an anonymous function: the syntax is <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code> where body must return a value</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4-11}
    Given the red checkbox can be located by id "red"
     When I navigate to "https://automationintesting.com/selenium/testpage"
      And I click the red checkbox
      And I capture my favorite color in the red checkbox by js
          """
          (function() {
            var color = element.value
            if (!element.checked) color = "Blue"
            return color;
          })()
          """
     Then my favorite color should be "Red"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-name-of-element-by-javascript-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-base64-decode-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I base64 decode <element>
  ```
  <p>Base64 decodes the text in the given element and binds the result to the same name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element containing the text to decode</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the data can be located by class "encoded-data"
     When I base64 decode the data
     Then the data should be "some binary data"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-base64-decode-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-base64-decode-element-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I base64 decode <element> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Base64 decodes the text in the given element and binds the result to the give name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element containing the text to decode</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name to bind the decoded value to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    Given the encoded data field can be located by class "encoded-data"
     When I base64 decode the encoded data as the decoded data
     Then the decoded data should be "some binary data"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-base64-decode-element-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-highlight-or-locate-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <highlight|locate> <element>
  ```
  <p>Locates and highlights the given element on the current page.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;highlight|locate&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>highlight</code> or <code>locate</code></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I locate the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-highlight-or-locate-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

### Then

<details id="element-should-be-state">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] be <state>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not an element is in a given state.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] be <state>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] be <state> with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] be <state> with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the state if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;state&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>displayed</code> to check if the element is displayed</li>
        <li><code>hidden</code> to check if the element is not displayed</li>
        <li><code>checked</code> (or <code>ticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to check if a checkbox is ticked</li>
        <li><code>unchecked</code> (or <code>unticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to check if a checkbox is not ticked</li>
        <li><code>enabled</code> to check if the element is enabled</li>
        <li><code>disabled</code> to check if the element is disabled</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     Then my todo list should not be displayed
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-should-be-state">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the text value of an element matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> "<expression>" with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> "<expression>" with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I enter "Get the milk" in the todo field
     Then my todo list should contain "Get the milk"
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="element-should-match-expression-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```

  <p>Checks whether or not the text value of an element matches a referenced expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <element> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to check</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an expression value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {6}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
      And my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
      And my item is "Feed the cat"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I enter my item in the todo field
     Then my todo list should contain my item
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#element-should-match-expression-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="drodown-text-or-value-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] be blank
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not a dropdown selection matches a blank string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] be blank with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] be blank with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the dropdown element to check</li>
    <li><code>&lt;text|value&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to check the displayed text of the selection</li>
        <li><code>value</code> to check the option value of the selection</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select the 2nd option in the age dropdown
     Then the age dropdown value should not be blank
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#drodown-text-or-value-should-match-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.26.0">v3.26.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="drodown-text-or-value-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not a dropdown selection matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the dropdown element to check</li>
    <li><code>&lt;text|value&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to check the displayed text of the selection</li>
        <li><code>value</code> to check the option value of the selection</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select the 2nd option in the age dropdown
     Then the age dropdown value should be "18"
  ```
