<details id="drodown-text-or-value-should-match-expression-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not a dropdown selection matches a referenced expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  <dropdown> <text|value> should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;dropdown&gt;</code> is the dropdown element to check</li>
    <li><code>&lt;text|value&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>text</code> to check the displayed text of the selection</li>
        <li><code>value</code> to check the option value of the selection</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an expression value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the age dropdown can be located by id "challenger_age"
      And my age is "18"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/step/2"
      And I select the 2nd option in the age dropdown
     Then the age dropdown value should be my age
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#drodown-text-or-value-should-match-expression-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

## Windows and tabs

### Given

<details id="i-have-an-open-browser">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I have an open browser
  ```
  <p>Opens a browser if none are open</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given I have an open browser
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     Then I should have 1 open browser
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-have-an-open-browser">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.41.0">v2.41.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-have-no-open-browser">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I have no open browser
  ```
  <p>Closes all open browsers</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1}
    Given I have no open browser
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     Then I should have 1 open browser
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-have-no-open-browser">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.41.0">v2.41.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

### When

<details id="i-start-a-new-browser">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I start a new browser
  ```
  <p>Starts a new browser session (or switches to exising one if it is already open).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
   Given I have no open browser
    When I start a new browser
    Then I should have 1 open browser
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-start-a-new-browser">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-close-the-current-browser">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I close the[ current] browser
  ```
  <p>Closes the current browser session (or does nothing if one is not open).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>[ current]</code> including the word <code>current</code> is optional and makes no difference, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.3.0">v1.3.0</Link></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2,4}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     And I close the current browser
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/vue/"
     And I close the browser
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-close-the-current-browser">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-start-a-browser-for-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I start a browser for <name>
  ```
  <p>Starts a new browser session with the given name (closes any existing browser of that name first).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is a name assigned to the browser session</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1,3}
    When I start a browser for React
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     And I start a browser for Vue
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/vue/"
    Then I should have 2 open browsers
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-start-a-browser-for-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to <name>
  ```
  <p>Switches to a named browser session (starts a new browser if one of that name is not already open). All browser actions performed after this will execute in the named session.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the browser session to switch to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    When I start a browser for React
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     And I start a browser for Vue
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/vue/"
     And I switch to React
    Then the current URL should contain "react"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-close-the-browser-for-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I close the browser for <name>
  ```
  <p>Closes a named browser session (does nothing if one of that name is not open).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> is the name of the browser session to close</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    When I start a browser for React
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     And I close the browser for React
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-close-the-browser-for-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.2.0">v1.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-the-default-content">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to the default content
  ```
  <p>Switches from an iframe to the default or main content window.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://page-with-iframes"
     And I switch to the default content
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-the-default-content">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-start-a-new-browser-tab-or-window">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I start a new browser <tab|window>
  ```
  <p>Starts a new browser tab or window (or starts a new browser session if one is not open).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://google.com"
     And I start a new browser tab
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-start-a-new-browser-tab-or-window">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.0.0">v3.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-tab-or-window-occurrence">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to <tab|window> <occurrence>
  ```
  <p>Switches to a previously opened tab or window occurrence.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;occurrence&gt;</code> is the tab or window occurrence to switch to (1st opened is occurrence 1, 2nd is 2, ..)
      <ul>
        <li><em>Note:</em> the occurrence number of the default tab/window in a new browser session is 0</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    When I navigate to "https://google.com"
     And I start a new browser tab
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     And I switch to window 1
    Then the page title should contain "Google"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-tab-or-window-occurrence">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.0.0">v3.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-close-tab-or-window-occurrence">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I close <tab|window> <occurrence>
  ```
  <p>Closes a previously opened tab or window occurrence.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;occurrence&gt;</code> is the tab or window occurrence to close to (1st opened is occurrence 1, 2nd is 2, ..)
      <ul>
        <li><em>Note:</em> you cannot close the default tab/window opened by starting a new browser session with this DSL. Use <Link to="#i-close-the-current-browser"><code>I close the[ current] browser</code></Link> instead in that case.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    When I navigate to "https://google.com"
     And I start a new browser tab
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     And I close tab 1
    Then the page title should contain "Google"
  ```
  
  If used in conjunction with <Link to="/docs/advanced/try-steps"><code>@Try</code></Link>, will switch to the parent window regardless of whether or not a tab or window was closed (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.4">3.12.4</Link>).
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-close-tab-or-window-occurrence">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.0.0">v3.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-the-child-tab-or-window">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to the child <tab|window>
  ```
  <p>Switches to the most recently opened child tab or window (without closing the parent window)</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the new window button can be located by name "newbrowserwindow123"
     When I navigate to "https://nxtgenaiacademy.com/multiplewindows/"
      And I click the new window button
      And I switch to the child window
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-the-child-tab-or-window">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-close-the-child-tab-or-window">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I close the child <tab|window>
  ```
  <p>Closes the currently active child tab or window and passes control back to the parent window.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the new tab button can be located by name "newbrowsertab453"
     When I navigate to "https://nxtgenaiacademy.com/multiplewindows/"
      And I click the new tab button
      And I switch to the child tab
      And I close the child tab
  ```
  
  If used in conjunction with <Link to="/docs/advanced/try-steps"><code>@Try</code></Link>, will switch to the parent window regardless of whether or not a child window was closed (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.4">3.12.4</Link>).
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-close-the-child-tab-or-window">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-child-tab-or-window-occurrence">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to child <tab|window> <occurrence>
  ```
  <p>Switches to a child tab or window occurrence (without closing the parent window).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;occurrence&gt;</code> is the tab or window occurrence to switch to (1st opened is occurrence 1, 2nd is 2, ..)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the new window button can be located by name "newbrowserwindow123"
     When I navigate to "https://nxtgenaiacademy.com/multiplewindows/"
      And I click the new window button
      And I switch to child window 1
  ```
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-child-tab-or-window-occurrence">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.49.0">v2.49.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-close-child-tab-or-window-occurrence">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I close child <tab|window> <occurrence>
  ```
  <p>Closes a child tab or window occurrence and passes control back to the parent window.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
    <li><code>&lt;occurrence&gt;</code> is the tab or window occurrence to close (1st opened is occurrence 1, 2nd is 2, ..)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the new tab button can be located by name "newbrowsertab453"
     When I navigate to "https://nxtgenaiacademy.com/multiplewindows/"
      And I click the new tab button
      And I switch to child tab 1
      And I close child tab 1
  ```

  If used in conjunction with <Link to="/docs/advanced/try-steps"><code>@Try</code></Link>, will switch to the parent window regardless of whether or not a child window was closed (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.12.4">3.12.4</Link>).
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-close-child-tab-or-window-occurrence">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.49.0">v2.49.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-switch-to-the-parent-tab-or-window">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I switch to the <parent|root> <tab|window>
  ```
  <p>Switches to the parent window (without closing the currently active child window).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;parent|root&gt;</code> is either <code>parent</code> (or <code>root</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.49.0">v2.49.0</Link>)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;tab|window&gt;</code> is either <code>tab</code> or <code>window</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the new window button can be located by name "newbrowserwindow123"
     When I navigate to "https://nxtgenaiacademy.com/multiplewindows/"
      And I click the new window button
      And I switch to child window 1
      And I switch to the parent window
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-switch-to-the-parent-tab-or-window">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-maximize-the-window">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <maximize|maximise> the window
  ```
  <p>Maximizes the currently active browser window to fill the entire screen area.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;maximize|maximise&gt;</code> is either <code>maximize</code> or <code>maximise</code> (makes no difference)</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     And I maximize the window
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-maximize-the-window">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.2.0">v2.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-resize-the-window-to-width-w-and-height-h">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I resize the window to width <w> and height <h>
  ```
  <p>Resizes the currently active browser window to the given dimensions.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;w&gt;</code> is the width in pixels</li>
    <li><code>&lt;h&gt;</code> is the height in pixels</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     And I resize the window to width 1280 and height 720
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-resize-the-window-to-width-w-and-height-h">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.2.0">v2.2.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-send-keys">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I send "<keys>"
  ```
  <p>Sends a sequence of keys to the browser (for emulating keyboard shortcuts).</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;keys&gt;</code> is a <code>,</code> or <code>+</code> (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link>) separated list of keys to send.
      <ul>
        <li>Keys can be single keyboard characters or any supported <Link to="https://seleniumhq.github.io/selenium/docs/api/java/org/openqa/selenium/Keys.html">key constants</Link></li>
        <li><i>Note:</i> Keys behave differently on different platforms</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
     When I navigate to "https://google.com"
      And I send "COMMAND+t"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-send-keys">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.44.0">v2.44.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>


### Then

<details id="i-should-have-1-open-browser">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I should have 1 open browser
  ```
  <p>Checks that only one browser session is currently open. Reports an assertion error if not.</p>
  </summary>

  <p>

  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  I should have 1 open browser  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```
  
  </p>

  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
   Given I have no open browser
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
    Then I should have 1 open browser
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-should-have-1-open-browser">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.41.0">v2.41.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-should-have-count-open-browsers">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I should have <count> open browsers
  ```
  <p>Checks that a given number of browsers are currently open. Reports an assertion error if not.</p>
  </summary>

  <p>

  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  I should have <count> open browsers  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>

  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>count</code> the expected number of open browsers</li>
  </ul>

  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
   Given I have no open browser
    When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
     And I start a browser for Vue
     And I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/vue"
    Then I should have 2 open browsers
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-should-have-count-open-browsers">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.41.0">v2.41.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

## Alerts and popups

### When

<details id="i-accept-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I accept the <alert|confirmation> popup
  ```
  <p>Accepts and closes an alert or confirmation popup by clicking OK.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;alert|confirmation&gt;</code> is either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>alert</code> for an alert box with an OK button</li>
        <li><code>confirmation</code> for a confirmation box with OK and Cancel buttons</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the alert button can be located by css ".btn" at index 0
     When I navigate to "https://www.seleniumeasy.com/test/javascript-alert-box-demo.html"
      And I click the alert button
      And I accept the alert popup
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-accept-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-dismiss-the-confirmation-popup">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I dismiss the confirmation popup
  ```
  <p>Dismisses and closes a confirmation popup by clicking Cancel.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the confirmation button can be located by css ".btn" at index 1
     When I navigate to "https://www.seleniumeasy.com/test/javascript-alert-box-demo.html"
      And I click the confirmation button
      And I dismiss the confirmation popup
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-dismiss-the-confirmation-popup">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the <alert|confirmation> popup message
  ```
  <p>Captures the alert or confirmation popup message and binds it to <code>the &lt;alert|confirmation&gt; popup message</code> in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;alert|confirmation&gt;</code> is either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>alert</code> for an alert box with an OK button</li>
        <li><code>confirmation</code> for a confirmation box with OK and Cancel buttons</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the alert button can be located by css ".btn" at index 0
     When I navigate to "https://www.seleniumeasy.com/test/javascript-alert-box-demo.html"
      And I click the alert button
      And I capture the alert popup message
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.24.0">v2.24.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the <alert|confirmation> popup message as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the alert or confirmation popup message and binds it to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;alert|confirmation&gt;</code> is either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>alert</code> for an alert box with an OK button</li>
        <li><code>confirmation</code> for a confirmation box with OK and Cancel buttons</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the confirmation button can be located by css ".btn" at index 1
     When I navigate to "https://www.seleniumeasy.com/test/javascript-alert-box-demo.html"
      And I click the confirmation button
      And I capture the confirmation popup message as the alert message
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.24.0">v2.24.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

### Then

<details id="the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-blank">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] be blank
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the message in the alert or confirmation popup box matches a blank string. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] be blank  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] be blank with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] be blank with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the alert button can be located by css ".btn" at index 0
     When I navigate to "https://www.seleniumeasy.com/test/javascript-alert-box-demo.html"
      And I click the alert button
     Then the alert popup message should not be blank
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-blank">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.26.0">v3.26.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>


<details id="the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-expression">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> "<expression>"
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the message in the alert or confirmation popup box matches a given expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> "<expression>"  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> "<expression>" with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> "<expression>" with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the expression to match (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the alert button can be located by css ".btn" at index 0
     When I navigate to "https://www.seleniumeasy.com/test/javascript-alert-box-demo.html"
      And I click the alert button
     Then the alert popup message should be "I am an alert box!"
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-expression">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.24.0">v2.24.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-expression-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>
  ```
  
  <p>Checks whether or not the message in the alert or confirmation popup box matches a referenced expression. Reports an assertion error if the match fails.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom assertion error message (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.9.0">v3.9.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> <expressionRef>  @Message("my custom assert fail message")
  ```

  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with no timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with no <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <hr/>
  <p>
  <p>Or with custom timeout (as of <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.41.0">v3.41.0</Link>):</p>

  ```gherkin
  the <alert|confirmation> popup message should[ not] <match> <expressionRef> with <timeoutSecs> second <wait|timeout>
  ```
  
  </p>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the match if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;match&gt;</code> is the type of match to perform, one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>be</code> for exact match</li>
        <li><code>contain</code> for partial match</li>
        <li><code>start with</code> for partial leading match</li>
        <li><code>end with</code> for partial trailing match</li>
        <li><code>match regex</code> for regex match</li>
        <li><code>match xpath</code> for XML match</li>
        <li><code>match json path</code> for <Link to="https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath/blob/master/README.md">JSON match</Link>, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.4.0">v1.4.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>match template file</code> for <Link to="/docs/advanced/template-matching">template</Link> file match, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.16.0">v2.16.0</Link></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;expressionRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the expression to match
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to an expression value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutSecs&gt;</code> is the timeout period in seconds</li>
    <li><code>&lt;wait|timeout&gt;</code> is either <code>wait</code> or <code>timeout</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given the confirmation button can be located by css ".btn" at index 1
      And the expected message is "Press a button!"
     When I navigate to "https://www.seleniumeasy.com/test/javascript-alert-box-demo.html"
      And I click the confirmation button
     Then the confirmation popup message should be the expected message
  ```
  
  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#the-alert-or-confirmation-popup-message-should-match-expression-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.24.0">v2.24.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

## Screenshots

### When

<details id="i-capture-the-current-screenshot">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the current screenshot
  ```
  <p>Captures the current screenshot and attaches it to the Gwen report.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I capture the current screenshot
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-current-screenshot">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.6.0">v1.6.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-the-current-screenshot-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture the current screenshot as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the current screenshot, attaches it to the Gwen report, and binds the filepath of the saved image to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> the name to bind the captured image filepath to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I enter "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I capture the current screenshot as the screenshot image
     Then the screenshot image should contain "path/to/image.png"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-the-current-screenshot-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.49.0">v2.49.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

#### Element level screenshots

<details id="i-capture-element-screenshot-of-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture element screenshot of <element>
  ```
  <p>Captures the screenshot of a web element and attaches it to the Gwen report.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> the name of the web element to capture the screenshot of</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I type "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I capture element screenshot of the todo field
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-element-screenshot-of-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.0.0">v3.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-capture-element-screenshot-of-element-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I capture element screenshot of <element> as <name>
  ```
  <p>Captures the screenshot of a web element, attaches it to the Gwen report, and binds the filepath of the saved image to the given name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> the name of the web element to capture the screenshot of</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> the name to bind the captured image filepath to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I type "Walk the dog" in the todo field
      And I capture element screenshot of the todo field as my element screenshot
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-capture-element-screenshot-of-element-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.0.0">v3.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

## Files

### When

<details id="i-attach-filepath-as-name">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I attach "<filepath>" as "<name>"
  ```
  or since v3.0.0
  ```gherkin
  I attach "<filepath>" as <name>
  ```

  <p>Attaches a local file to the Gwen report and assigns it a name. The link to the attachment in the report will have the given name.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the local file to attach</li>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code> the name to assign to the file attachment</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
     When I attach "path/to/data.csv" as "data"
  ```
  Or since <Link to="/docs/gwen3">Gwen 3</Link>

  ```gherkin
     When I attach "path/to/data.csv" as data
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-attach-filepath-as-name">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.52.0">v2.52.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-write-append-text-to-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> "<text>" to "<filepath>" file
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends text to a file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with the provided text</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append the provided text to existing content in file</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> the text to write or append to the file</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the local file to write or append the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
     When I write "Gwen automation" to "path/to/file.txt" file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-write-append-text-to-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.25.0">v3.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-write-append-text-ref-to-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> <textRef> to "<filepath>" file
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends a text reference value to a file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with the provided text</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append the provided text to existing content in file</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to write or append to the file
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the local file to write or append the text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {6}
     Given my content is
           """
           Gwen automation and robotics
           for Gherkin
           """
     When I write my content to "path/to/file.txt" file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-write-append-text-ref-to-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.25.0">v3.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-write-append-new-line-to-file">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> new line to "<filepath>" file
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends a new line to a file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with a new line</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append a new line to existing content in file</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the local file to write or append the new line to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
     When I append new line to "path/to/file.txt" file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-write-append-new-line-to-file">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.25.0">v3.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-write-append-text-to-file-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> "<text>" to <filepathRef> file
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends text to a referenced file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with the provided text</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append the provided text to existing content in file</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;text&gt;</code> the text to write or append to the file</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file to write or append the provided text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
     Given my file is "path/to/file.txt"
      When I append "Gwen automation" to my file
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-write-append-text-to-file-ref">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.25.0">v3.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-write-append-text-ref-to-file-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> <textRef> to <filepathRef> file
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends a text reference value to a referenced file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with the provided text</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append the provided text to existing content in file</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;textRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the text to write or append to the file
      <ul>
        <li>Can be the name of any binding that contains or resolves to a text value, including a web element in which case the text in the element will be dynamically retrieved and used.</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepathRef&gt;</code> is the name of the binding containing the path of the file to write or append the provided text to</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {7}
     Given my file is "path/to/file.txt"
       And my content is
           """
           Gwen automation and robotics
           for Gherkin
           """
     When I write my content to my file
  ```

    <div align="center"></div>

  </div>

<details id="i-write-append-new-line-to-file-ref">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I <write|append> new line to <filepathRef> file
  ```
  <p>Writes or appends a new line to a referenced file.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;write|append&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>&lt;write&gt;</code> to overwrite entire content of file with a new line</li>
        <li><code>&lt;append&gt;</code> to append a new line to existing content in file</li>

</details>

## Sleeps and waits

### Given

<details id="i-wait-duration-seconds-when-element-is-actioned">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait <duration> second[s] when <element> is <actioned>
  ```
  <p>Triggers a sleep for a given number of seconds whenever a specific action is performed on an element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;duration&gt;</code> is the number of seconds to sleep</li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> the name of the web element</li>
    <li><code>&lt;actioned&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>clicked</code> to sleep when the element is clicked</li>
        <li><code>right clicked</code> to sleep when the element is right clicked, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>double clicked</code> to sleep when the element is double clicked, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>submitted</code> to sleep when the form element is submitted</li>
        <li><code>checked</code> (or <code>ticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to sleep when the checkbox element is ticked</li>
        <li><code>unchecked</code> (or <code>unticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to sleep when the checkbox element is unticked</li>
        <li><code>selected</code> to sleep when a dropdown option is selected in the element</li>
        <li><code>deselected</code> to sleep when a mutli-select dropdown option is deselected in the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>typed</code> to sleep when text is typed into the element</li>
        <li><code>entered</code> to sleep when text is entered into the element</li>
        <li><code>cleared</code> to sleep when the text is cleared in the element</li>
        <li><code>moved to</code> to sleep when the focus is moved to the element</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>Include <code>s</code> after <code>second</code> when specifying a <code>&lt;duration&gt;</code> that is not 1, omit otherwise</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {2}
  Given the submit button can be located by id "submit"
    And I wait 3 seconds when the submit button is clicked
   When I navigate to "${token.website}"
    And I click the submit button
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-duration-seconds-when-element-is-actioned">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-condition-when-element-is-actioned">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until <condition> when <element> is <actioned>
  ```
  <p>Triggers a wait for a condition whenever a specific action is performed on an element.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;condition&gt;</code> the name of a binding containing a javascript function or expression that will return true when the condition is satisfied and false when it is not</li>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> the name of the web element</li>
    <li><code>&lt;actioned&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>clicked</code> to wait when the element is clicked</li>
        <li><code>right clicked</code> to wait when the element is right clicked, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.8.0">v2.8.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>double clicked</code> to wait when the element is double clicked, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.12.0">v2.12.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>submitted</code> to wait when the form element is submitted</li>
        <li><code>checked</code> (or <code>ticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to wait when the checkbox element is ticked</li>
        <li><code>unchecked</code> (or <code>unticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to wait when the checkbox element is unticked</li>
        <li><code>selected</code> to wait when a dropdown option is selected in the element</li>
        <li><code>deselected</code> to wait when a mutli-select dropdown option is deselected in the element, since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.13.0">v2.13.0</Link></li>
        <li><code>typed</code> to wait when text is typed into the element</li>
        <li><code>entered</code> to wait when text is entered into the element</li>
        <li><code>cleared</code> to wait when the text is cleared in the element</li>
        <li><code>moved to</code> to wait when the focus is moved to the element</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li>Include <code>s</code> after <code>second</code> when specifying a <code>&lt;duration&gt;</code> that is not 1, omit otherwise</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the submit button can be located by name "submit"
      And the token field can be located by class "token"
      And the submit button is displayed is defined by javascript "!!document.getElementById('submit')"
      And I wait until the submit button is displayed when the token field is entered
     When I navigate to "${token.website}"
      And I enter "my token" in the token field
      And I click the submit button
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-condition-when-element-is-actioned">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

### When

<details id="i-wait-for-element">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait for <element>
  ```
  <p>Waits for an element to appear on a page for a default number of seconds before timing out.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to wait for</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # Wait for a dynamically rendered input field 
    Given the dynamic input field can be located by tag "input"
     When I wait for the dynamic input field
     Then the dynamic input field should be displayed
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-for-element">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-for-element-for-duration-seconds">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait for <element> for <duration> second[s]
  ```
  <p>Waits for an element to appear on a page for a given number of seconds before timing out.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to wait for</li>
    <li><code>&lt;duration&gt;</code> is the number of seconds to wait before timing out</li>
    <li>Include trailing <code>s</code> when specifying a <code>&lt;duration&gt;</code> that is not 1, omit otherwise</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # Wait for a dynamically rendered input field 
    Given the dynamic input field can be located by tag "input"
     When I wait for the dynamic input field for 3 seconds
     Then the dynamic input field should be displayed
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-for-element-for-duration-seconds">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-for-element-text">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait for <element> text
  ```
  <p>Waits for the text of an element to appear on a page for a default number of seconds before timing out.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to wait for the text to appear</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # Wait for a dynamically displayed token
    Given the one time token can be located by javascript "$('.token').get(0)"
     When I wait for the one time token text
      And I capture the one time token
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-for-element-text">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-for-element-text-for-duration-seconds">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait for <element> text for <duration> second[s]
  ```
  <p>Waits for the text of an element to appear on a page for a given number of seconds before timing out.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to wait for the text to appear</li>
    <li><code>&lt;duration&gt;</code> is the number of seconds to wait before timing out</li>
    <li>Include trailing <code>s</code> when specifying a <code>&lt;duration&gt;</code> that is not 1, omit otherwise</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    # Wait for a dynamically displayed token
    Given the one time token can be located by javascript "$('.token').get(0)"
     When I wait for the one time token text for 3 seconds
      And I capture the one time token
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-for-element-text-for-duration-seconds">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-element-is-state">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until <element> is[ not] <state>
  ```
  <p>Waits for an element to transition to a given state.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;element&gt;</code> is the name of the element to wait for</li>
    <li><code>not</code> negates the state if included</li>
    <li><code>&lt;state&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>displayed</code> to wait until the element is displayed</li>
        <li><code>hidden</code> to wait until the element is not displayed</li>
        <li><code>checked</code> (or <code>ticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to wait until a checkbox is ticked</li>
        <li><code>unchecked</code> (or <code>unticked</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.4.0">v2.4.0</Link>) to wait until a checkbox is not ticked</li>
        <li><code>enabled</code> to wait until the element is enabled</li>
        <li><code>disabled</code> to wait until the element is disabled</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {5}
    Given my todo list can be located by css ".todo-list"
      And the todo field can be located by class "new-todo"
     When I navigate to "https://todomvc.com/examples/react"
      And I enter "Get the milk" in the todo field
      And I wait until my todo list is displayed
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-element-is-state">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.25.0">v2.25.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-javascript">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until "<javascript>"
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly executes the given javascript expression or anonymous function until true is returned using no delay interval and default timeout period. The default timeout period is equal to the configured <code>gwen.web.wait.seconds</code> setting value.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or anonymous function returning a boolean value (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>For an expression: no <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>For an anonymous function: the syntax is <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code> where body must return a boolean</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
   Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
    When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
     And I wait until "!!$('h1')"
    Then the heading should be "Welcome to our Script Challenge"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-javascript">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-javascript-using-delay">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until "<javascript>" using <delay> <delayUnit> delay
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly executes the given javascript expression or anonymous function until true is returned using the given delay interval and default timeout period. The default timeout period is equal to the configured <code>gwen.web.wait.seconds</code> setting value.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or anonymous function returning a boolean value
      <ul>
        <li>For an expression: no <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>For an anonymous function: the syntax is <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code> where body must return a boolean</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;delay&gt;</code> is the delay period between repetitive checks</li>
    <li><code>&lt;delayUnit&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>second</code></li>
        <li><code>millisecond</code></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
      And I wait until "!!$('h1')" using 200 millisecond delay
     Then the heading should be "Welcome to our Script Challenge"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-javascript-using-delay">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-javascript-using-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until "<javascript>" using <timeout> <timeoutUnit> timeout
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly executes the given javascript expression or anonymous function until true is returned using no delay interval and the given timeout period.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or anonymous function returning a boolean value
      <ul>
        <li>For an expression: no <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>For an anonymous function: the syntax is <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code> where body must return a boolean</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeout&gt;</code> is the timeout period</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutUnit&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>minute</code></li>
        <li><code>second</code></li>
        <li><code>millisecond</code></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
      And I wait until "!!$('h1')" using 3 second timeout
     Then the heading should be "Welcome to our Script Challenge"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-javascript-using-timeout">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>


<details id="i-wait-until-javascript-using-delay-and-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until "<javascript>" using <delay> <delayUnit> delay and <timeout> <timeoutUnit> timeout
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly executes the given javascript expression or anonymous function until true is returned using the given delay interval and timeout period.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript&gt;</code> is the javascript expression or anonymous function returning a boolean value
      <ul>
        <li>For an expression: no <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>For an anonymous function: the syntax is <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code> where body must return a boolean</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;delay&gt;</code> is the delay period between repetitive checks</li>
    <li><code>&lt;delayUnit&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>second</code></li>
        <li><code>millisecond</code></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeout&gt;</code> is the timeout period</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutUnit&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>minute</code></li>
        <li><code>second</code></li>
        <li><code>millisecond</code></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {3}
    Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
      And I wait until "!!$('h1')" using 250 millisecond delay and 3 second timeout
     Then the heading should be "Welcome to our Script Challenge"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-javascript-using-delay-and-timeout">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-condition">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until <condition>
  ```
  <p>Waits until a condition is satisfied.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;condition&gt;</code> is the name of a binding containing a javascript function or expression that will return true when the condition is satisfied and false when it is not</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
   Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
     And the heading is displayed is defined by javascript "!!$('h1')"
    When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
     And I wait until the heading is displayed
    Then the heading should be "Welcome to our Script Challenge"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-condition">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-condition-using-delay">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until <condition> using <delay> <delayUnit> delay
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly waits until the given condition is satisfied using the given delay interval and default timeout period. The default timeout period is equal to the configured <code>gwen.web.wait.seconds</code> setting value.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;condition&gt;</code> is the name of a binding containing a javascript function or expression that will return true when the condition is satisfied and false when it is not</li>
    <li><code>&lt;delay&gt;</code> is the delay period between repetitive checks</li>
    <li><code>&lt;delayUnit&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>second</code></li>
        <li><code>millisecond</code></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
      And the heading is displayed is defined by javascript "!!$('h1')"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
      And I wait until the heading is displayed using 200 millisecond delay
     Then the heading should be "Welcome to our Script Challenge"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-condition-using-delay">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-condition-using-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until <condition> using <timeout> <timeoutUnit> timeout
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly waits until the given condition is satisfied using no delay interval and the given timeout period.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;condition&gt;</code> is the name of a binding containing a javascript function or expression that will return true when the condition is satisfied and false when it is not</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeout&gt;</code> is the timeout period</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutUnit&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>minute</code></li>
        <li><code>second</code></li>
        <li><code>millisecond</code></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
      And the heading is displayed is defined by javascript "!!$('h1')"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
      And I wait until the heading is displayed using 3 second timeout
     Then the heading should be "Welcome to our Script Challenge"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-condition-using-timeout">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-until-condition-using-delay-and-timeout">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait until <condition> using <delay> <delayUnit> delay and <timeout> <timeoutUnit> timeout
  ```
  <p>Repeatedly waits until the given condition is satisfied using the given delay interval and timeout period.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;condition&gt;</code> is the name of a binding containing a javascript function or expression that will return true when the condition is satisfied and false when it is not</li>
    <li><code>&lt;delay&gt;</code> is the delay period between repetitive checks</li>
    <li><code>&lt;delayUnit&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>second</code></li>
        <li><code>millisecond</code></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeout&gt;</code> is the timeout period</li>
    <li><code>&lt;timeoutUnit&gt;</code> is one of:
      <ul>
        <li><code>minute</code></li>
        <li><code>second</code></li>
        <li><code>millisecond</code></li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {4}
    Given the heading can be located by tag "h1"
      And the heading is displayed is defined by javascript "!!$('h1')"
     When I navigate to "https://challengers.flood.io/start"
      And I wait until the heading is displayed using 250 millisecond delay and 3 second timeout
     Then the heading should be "Welcome to our Script Challenge"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-until-condition-using-delay-and-timeout">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-wait-duration-seconds">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I wait <duration> second[s]
  ```
  <p>Sleeps for the given number of seconds.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;duration&gt;</code> is the number of seconds to sleep</li>
    <li>Include trailing <code>s</code> when specifying a <code>&lt;duration&gt;</code> that is not 1, omit otherwise</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I wait for 5 seconds
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-wait-duration-seconds">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

## Scripts and processes

### When

<details id="i-execute-javascript">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I execute <javascript|js> "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a JavaScript expression or anonymous function.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;javascript|js&gt;</code> is <code>javascript</code> (or <code>js</code> since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.46.0">v2.46.0</Link>)</li>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the JavaScript expression or anonymous function to execute (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>For an anonymous function: the syntax is <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code> where body must return a value</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I execute js "alert('Hello Gwen World')"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-execute-javascript">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.9.0">v2.9.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-execute-system-process">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I execute system process "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a local system process or script.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the system process or script to execute</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I execute system process "echo 'Hello Gwen World'"
     And I execute system process "path/to/script.bat"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-execute-system-process">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-execute-system-process-delimited-by-delimiters">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I execute system process "<expression>" delimited by "<delimiters>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a delimited local system process or script.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> the delimited system process to execute
      <ul>
        <li>Delmiters are required for special cases such as when unbalanced quoted strings are passed as arguments (see example).</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;delmiters&gt;</code> is a regex pattern defining the delimiter(s) used in <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I execute system process "echo,"quoted text " and orphan quote"" delimited by ","
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-execute-system-process-delimited-by-delimiters">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-execute-a-unix-system-process">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I execute a unix system process "<expression>"
  ```
  or since v3.14.2
  ```gherkin
  I execute unix system process "<expression>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a local unix system process or shell script.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> is the system process or script to execute</li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin {1,2}
    When I execute a unix system process "echo 'Hello Gwen World'"
     And I execute a unix system process "./path/to/script.sh"
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-execute-a-unix-system-process">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v1.0.0">v1.0.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

<details id="i-execute-a-unix-system-process-delimited-by-delimiters">
  <summary class="dsl">

  <b>Dropped</b> since v3.19.0

  ```gherkin
  I execute a unix system process "<expression>" delimited by "<delimiters>"
  ```
  or since v3.14.2
  ```gherkin
  I execute unix system process "<expression>" delimited by "<delimiters>"
  ```
  <p>Executes a delimited local unix system process or script.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;expression&gt;</code> the delimited system process to execute
      <ul>
        <li>Delmiters are required for special cases such as when unbalanced quoted strings are passed as arguments (see example).</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
    <li><code>&lt;delmiters&gt;</code> is a regex pattern defining the delimiter(s) used in <code>&lt;expression&gt;</code></li>
  </ul>
  <p>Example</p>

  ```gherkin
    When I execute a unix system process "echo,"quoted text " and orphan quote"" delimited by ","
  ```

  <div class="grid-3">
    <div><Link to="#i-execute-a-unix-system-process-delimited-by-delimiters">Link</Link></div>
    <div align="center"></div>
    <div align="right">Since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v2.53.0">v2.53.0</Link></div>
  </div>
</details>

## Data Lookups

<details id="i-lookup-name-in-the-filepath-file-where-filter">
  <summary class="dsl">

  ```gherkin
  I lookup <name> in the "<filepath>" file where "<predicate>"
  ```
  <p>Looks up a named data value in a CSV or JSON file based on a predicate function and binds its value to the same name in the global scope.</p>
  </summary>
  <p>Where</p>
  <ul>
    <li><code>&lt;name&gt;</code>the name of the data to look up the value of and the name to bind it to</li>
    <li><code>&lt;filepath&gt;</code> the path to the CSV or JSON file to look up</li>
    <li><code>&lt;predicate&gt;</code> is the javascript predicate expression or anonymous function that will return <code>true</code> when a match is found for a record or <code>false</code> otherwise (can be in <Link to="/docs/advanced/doc-strings">DocString</Link> position)
      <ul>
        <li>For an expression: no <code>return</code> prefix is required</li>
        <li>For an anonymous function: the syntax is <code>(function()&#123; body &#125;)()</code> where body must return a value</li>
      </ul>
      Data fields can be referenced in the predicate using either:
      <ul>
        <li><code>$&#123;data.record.NAME&#125;</code> (since <Link to="https://github.com/gwen-interpreter/gwen-web/releases/tag/v3.47.0">v3.47.0</Link>)</li>
        <li><code>$&#123;csv.record.NAME&#125;</code> for CSV data or <code>$&#123;json.record.NAME&#125;</code> for JSON data (for prior versions)</li>
      </ul>
    </li>
  </ul>
